INSTITUTE  (2ZZZGEL)                                              2202700100003 
           (1CANUBC) P.W.M.                                       2202700100004 
           (2BLGMOL) I.V P., F.P.                                 2202700100005 
REFERENCE  (J,PR/C,36,585,1987)                                   2202700100006 
           (W,MARTIN,1986)                                        2202700100007 
           (W,WEIGMANN,198603) Numerical data.                    2202700100008 
           (J,AIP,124,304,1985)                                   2202700100009 
AUTHOR     (H.Weigmann,P.W.Martin,R.Koehler,I.Van Parijs,         2202700100010 
            F.Poortmans,J.A.Wartena)                              2202700100011 
TITLE       Structure of unbound states in Si-29 from neutron     2202700100012 
            resonance spectroscopy of Si-28 + n                   2202700100013 
FACILITY   (LINAC,2ZZZGEL) Geel 150 MeV Electron Linac and the    2202700100014 
            high resolution neutron time-of-flight facility.      2202700100015 
            Pulsed beams with burst widths between 0.7 and 5 ns   2202700100016 
            at a repetition rate of 800 Hz were used.             2202700100017 
INC-SOURCE .White neutron source with mercury-cooled uranium      2202700100018 
            target.                                               2202700100019 
           .Beryllium-canned water moderators were used for the   2202700100020 
            capture measurements between 1 keV and 5 MeV.         2202700100021 
INC-SPECT  .White neutron spectrum.                               2202700100022 
           .A 2 cm thick uranium filter was used in the total     2202700100023 
            cross section measurements to reduce the gamma-       2202700100024 
            flash.                                                2202700100025 
           .A combination of uranium, lead and B4C filters was    2202700100026 
            used in the capture measurements to reduce the        2202700100027 
            gamma-flash and to prevent overlap of low energy      2202700100028 
            neutrons.                                             2202700100029 
SAMPLE     .A metallic silicon sample of natural composition      2202700100030 
            with a thickness of 0.07356 atoms/b was used for      2202700100031 
            the transmission measurements.                        2202700100032 
           .Cylindrical samples of the same composition with      2202700100033 
            8 cm diameter by 8 mm /0.04 nuclei/b/ or 16 mm        2202700100034 
            /0.07 nuclei/b/ thick, were used for the capture      2202700100035 
            measurements.                                         2202700100036 
METHOD     (TOF)                                                  2202700100037 
           .Flight path of 400 m used for total cross section     2202700100038 
            transmission measurements.                            2202700100039 
           .Flight path of 130 m used for capture measurements.   2202700100040 
DETECTOR   (SCIN) Two NE-110 scintillation detectors were used    2202700100041 
            for total cross section measurements, one of the      2202700100042 
            size 15 by 15 by 2 cm having a timing resolution of   2202700100043 
            1 ns, and the other 5 cm diameter by 2.5 cm thick     2202700100044 
            with a time resolution of 0.26 ns.                    2202700100045 
           (BGO) .Four 7.5 cm diameter by 7.5 cm thick bismuth-   2202700100046 
            germanate detectors, placed at 39, 90, 125 and 141    2202700100047 
            degrees with respect to the neutron beam direction,   2202700100048 
            were used for capture gamma-ray measurements.         2202700100049 
           (FISCH) An U-235 fission chamber placed at 30 m from   2202700100050 
            the target, was used for measuring the neutron flux   2202700100051 
            shape.                                                2202700100052 
ANALYSIS   .The total cross section data were analysed with the   2202700100053 
            multi-channel multi-level R-matrix code MULTI.        2202700100054 
           .The capture data were analysed with the area code     2202700100055 
            TACASI.                                               2202700100056 
           .The angular distributions of the capture gamma-rays   2202700100057 
            were used for spin and parity assignments.            2202700100058 
CORRECTION .The total cross section data were corrected for       2202700100059 
            dead-time and background in the TOF spectra. The      2202700100060 
            ratio background to signal was typically less than    2202700100061 
            0.1% in the region of 2 MeV, increasing to a value    2202700100062 
            of 2% at 19 MeV and 10% at 250 keV.                   2202700100063 
           .The capture data were corrected for the scattered     2202700100064 
            neutron background and the Compton contribution       2202700100065 
            from higher energy gamma-rays.                        2202700100066 
           .Resonance data were corrected for multiple scatter-   2202700100067 
            ing and self-shielding.                               2202700100068 
STATUS     .Data taken from the references given.                 2202700100069
